自然语言处理

[NLP-0] Recycled Attention: Efficient inference for long-context language models

【速读】： 该论文试图解决大型语言模型（LLMs）在处理长上下文输入时面临的计算负担问题，特别是每次生成步骤中对长序列输入进行注意力计算的瓶颈。解决方案的关键是提出了“循环注意力”（Recycled Attention）方法，该方法在推理时交替使用全上下文注意力和对输入标记子集的注意力。在执行部分注意力时，通过复用先前全注意力步骤中的注意力模式，仅关注前K个最相关的标记，从而减少了数据移动和注意力计算的成本。与仅关注局部上下文或高累积注意力分数的先前加速方法相比，该方法灵活地选择与当前解码步骤相关的标记。实验结果表明，该方法在保持性能的同时，实现了与仅考虑局部上下文的基线方法相当的加速效果，并进一步探索了基于查询相似性动态决定何时执行循环或全注意力步骤，以及通过循环注意力继续预训练模型的方法，以优化性能与效率的权衡。

链接: https://arxiv.org/abs/2411.05787
作者: Fangyuan Xu,Tanya Goyal,Eunsol Choi
关键词-EN: Generating long sequences, heavy computational burden, Generating long, attention, long-context input imposes
类目: Computation and Language (cs.CL)
备注:

点击查看摘要

Abstract:Generating long sequences of tokens given a long-context input imposes a heavy computational burden for large language models (LLMs). One of the computational bottleneck comes from computing attention over a long sequence of input at each generation step. In this paper, we propose Recycled Attention, an inference-time method which alternates between full context attention and attention over a subset of input tokens. When performing partial attention, we recycle the attention pattern of a previous token that has performed full attention and attend only to the top K most attended tokens, reducing the cost of data movement and attention computation. Compared to previously proposed inference-time acceleration method which attends only to local context or tokens with high accumulative attention scores, our approach flexibly chooses tokens that are relevant to the current decoding step. We evaluate our methods on RULER, a suite of tasks designed to comprehensively evaluate long-context abilities, and long-context language modeling tasks. Applying our method to off-the-shelf LLMs achieves comparable speedup to baselines which only consider local context while improving the performance by 2x. We further explore two ideas to improve performance-efficiency trade-offs: (1) dynamically decide when to perform recycled or full attention step based on the query similarities and (2) continued pre-training the model with Recycled Attention.
摘要：在给定长上下文输入的情况下生成长序列的 Token 对大语言模型 (LLM) 提出了沉重的计算负担。其中一个计算瓶颈来自于在每个生成步骤中对长输入序列进行注意力计算。本文提出了一种名为“循环注意力 (Recycled Attention)”的推理时方法，该方法在全上下文注意力和部分输入 Token 注意力之间交替进行。在执行部分注意力时，我们复用先前已进行全注意力计算的 Token 的注意力模式，仅对前 K 个最关注的 Token 进行注意力计算，从而减少了数据移动和注意力计算的成本。与先前提出的仅关注局部上下文或高累积注意力分数 Token 的推理时加速方法相比，我们的方法灵活地选择与当前解码步骤相关的 Token。我们在 RULER 上评估了我们的方法，RULER 是一套旨在全面评估长上下文能力的任务集，以及长上下文语言建模任务。将我们的方法应用于现成的 LLM 中，实现了与仅考虑局部上下文的基线相当的加速，同时性能提升了 2 倍。我们进一步探索了两种提高性能与效率权衡的方法：(1) 根据查询相似度动态决定何时执行循环或全注意力步骤；(2) 使用循环注意力继续预训练模型。

[NLP-1] ASL STEM Wiki: Dataset and Benchmark for Interpreting STEM Articles EMNLP2024

【速读】： 该论文试图解决聋人和听力障碍学生（DHH）在获取科学、技术、工程和数学（STEM）教育资源方面的显著障碍，特别是由于手语中STEM资源的稀缺性。解决方案的关键是引入了ASL STEM Wiki，这是一个包含254篇STEM主题的维基百科文章的平行语料库，这些文章被翻译成超过300小时的美国手语（ASL）。ASL STEM Wiki是首个专注于STEM的连续手语数据集，有助于开发用于ASL中STEM教育的AI资源。该数据集的一个关键应用是识别技术概念中频繁使用的指拼（fingerspelling），这种做法限制了DHH学生的学习能力。因此，论文开发了模型来识别指拼词，这些模型可以用于查询适当的手语符号，并向翻译者推荐，从而改善STEM教育资源的可访问性。

链接: https://arxiv.org/abs/2411.05783
作者: Kayo Yin,Chinmay Singh,Fyodor O. Minakov,Vanessa Milan,Hal Daumé III,Cyril Zhang,Alex X. Lu,Danielle Bragg
关键词-EN: ASL STEM Wiki, students face significant, face significant barriers, STEM Wiki, American Sign Language
类目: Computation and Language (cs.CL); Artificial Intelligence (cs.AI); Computer Vision and Pattern Recognition (cs.CV); Human-Computer Interaction (cs.HC)
备注: Accepted to EMNLP 2024

点击查看摘要

Abstract:Deaf and hard-of-hearing (DHH) students face significant barriers in accessing science, technology, engineering, and mathematics (STEM) education, notably due to the scarcity of STEM resources in signed languages. To help address this, we introduce ASL STEM Wiki: a parallel corpus of 254 Wikipedia articles on STEM topics in English, interpreted into over 300 hours of American Sign Language (ASL). ASL STEM Wiki is the first continuous signing dataset focused on STEM, facilitating the development of AI resources for STEM education in ASL. We identify several use cases of ASL STEM Wiki with human-centered applications. For example, because this dataset highlights the frequent use of fingerspelling for technical concepts, which inhibits DHH students’ ability to learn, we develop models to identify fingerspelled words – which can later be used to query for appropriate ASL signs to suggest to interpreters.
摘要：失聪和听力障碍（Deaf and Hard-of-Hearing, DHH）学生在获取科学、技术、工程和数学（Science, Technology, Engineering, and Mathematics, STEM）教育方面面临显著障碍，主要原因是手语中STEM资源的匮乏。为解决这一问题，我们推出了ASL STEM Wiki：一个包含254篇关于STEM主题的维基百科文章的平行语料库，这些文章被翻译成超过300小时的美国手语（American Sign Language, ASL）。ASL STEM Wiki是首个专注于STEM的连续手语数据集，有助于开发针对ASL的STEM教育AI资源。我们识别了ASL STEM Wiki在以人为中心的应用中的几个使用案例。例如，由于该数据集突显了技术概念中频繁使用的手指拼写（fingerspelling），这限制了DHH学生的学习能力，我们开发了模型来识别手指拼写的单词——这些模型后续可用于查询适当的手语符号，并向手语翻译员推荐。

[NLP-2] Using Language Models to Disambiguate Lexical Choices in Translation EMNLP2024

【速读】： 该论文试图解决翻译中词汇选择的问题，即源语言中的单一概念在目标语言中可能存在多种变体，需要通过上下文来确定最合适的变体。解决方案的关键在于创建了一个名为DTAiLS的数据集，该数据集包含了1,377个句子对，展示了从英语翻译到其他九种语言时的跨语言概念变异。通过评估最新的语言模型（LLMs）和神经机器翻译系统在DTAiLS上的表现，发现GPT-4在多种语言上达到了67%到85%的准确率。此外，论文还利用语言模型生成描述目标语言概念变异的英语规则，为较弱的模型提供高质量的词汇规则，显著提高了这些模型的准确率，甚至在某些情况下达到或超越了GPT-4的表现。

链接: https://arxiv.org/abs/2411.05781
作者: Josh Barua,Sanjay Subramanian,Kayo Yin,Alane Suhr
关键词-EN: single word, multiple variations, concept represented, Abstract, target language
类目: Computation and Language (cs.CL); Artificial Intelligence (cs.AI)
备注: Accepted to EMNLP 2024

点击查看摘要

Abstract:In translation, a concept represented by a single word in a source language can have multiple variations in a target language. The task of lexical selection requires using context to identify which variation is most appropriate for a source text. We work with native speakers of nine languages to create DTAiLS, a dataset of 1,377 sentence pairs that exhibit cross-lingual concept variation when translating from English. We evaluate recent LLMs and neural machine translation systems on DTAiLS, with the best-performing model, GPT-4, achieving from 67 to 85% accuracy across languages. Finally, we use language models to generate English rules describing target-language concept variations. Providing weaker models with high-quality lexical rules improves accuracy substantially, in some cases reaching or outperforming GPT-4.
摘要：在翻译过程中，源语言中由单个词表示的概念在目标语言中可能存在多种变体。词汇选择任务需要利用上下文来确定哪种变体最适合源文本。我们与九种语言的母语者合作，创建了DTAiLS数据集，该数据集包含1,377对句子，这些句子在从英语翻译时展示了跨语言概念变体。我们对最近的大语言模型和神经机器翻译系统在DTAiLS上进行了评估，表现最佳的模型GPT-4在不同语言中的准确率从67%到85%不等。最后，我们使用语言模型生成描述目标语言概念变体的英语规则。为较弱的模型提供高质量的词汇规则显著提高了准确性，在某些情况下达到了或超过了GPT-4的表现。

[NLP-3] LLM s as Method Actors: A Model for Prompt Engineering and Architecture

【速读】： 该论文试图解决的是如何提高大型语言模型（LLM）在解决复杂推理任务中的表现，特别是在《纽约时报》字谜游戏“Connections”中的表现。解决方案的关键在于引入“方法演员”（Method Actors）这一心理模型，将LLM视为演员，提示（prompts）视为剧本和提示，LLM的响应视为表演。通过这种模型，论文展示了在GPT-4o和OpenAI的o1-preview模型上，使用“方法演员”方法显著提升了LLM在解决“Connections”字谜游戏中的成功率，从传统的27%和“思维链”（Chain of Thoughts）方法的41%，提升到“方法演员”方法的86%，并且在o1-preview模型上，结合“方法演员”提示架构，将完美解决率从76%提高到87%。

链接: https://arxiv.org/abs/2411.05778
作者: Colin Doyle
关键词-EN: Method Actors, guiding LLM prompt, LLM prompt engineering, Method, mental model
类目: Artificial Intelligence (cs.AI); Computation and Language (cs.CL)
备注:

点击查看摘要

Abstract:We introduce “Method Actors” as a mental model for guiding LLM prompt engineering and prompt architecture. Under this mental model, LLMs should be thought of as actors; prompts as scripts and cues; and LLM responses as performances. We apply this mental model to the task of improving LLM performance at playing Connections, a New York Times word puzzle game that prior research identified as a challenging benchmark for evaluating LLM reasoning. Our experiments with GPT-4o show that a “Method Actors” approach can significantly improve LLM performance over both a vanilla and “Chain of Thoughts” approach. A vanilla approach solves 27% of Connections puzzles in our dataset and a “Chain of Thoughts” approach solves 41% of puzzles, whereas our strongest “Method Actor” approach solves 86% of puzzles. We also test OpenAI’s newest model designed specifically for complex reasoning tasks, o1-preview. When asked to solve a puzzle all at once, o1-preview solves 79% of Connections puzzles in our dataset, and when allowed to build puzzle solutions one guess at a time over multiple API calls, o1-preview solves 100% of the puzzles. Incorporating a “Method Actor” prompt architecture increases the percentage of puzzles that o1-preview solves perfectly from 76% to 87%.
摘要：我们提出了“方法演员”（Method Actors）作为一种心理模型，用于指导大语言模型（LLM）的提示工程和提示架构设计。在这个模型中，大语言模型应被视为演员；提示作为剧本和提示；而大语言模型的响应则被视为表演。我们将这一心理模型应用于提升大语言模型在玩“Connections”游戏中的表现，这是一个由《纽约时报》推出的字谜游戏，先前的研究表明它是一个评估大语言模型推理能力的具有挑战性的基准。我们的实验使用 GPT-4o 表明，“方法演员”方法可以显著提高大语言模型的表现，相比于传统的和“思维链”（Chain of Thoughts）方法。传统方法在我们的数据集中解决了27%的Connections谜题，“思维链”方法解决了41%的谜题，而我们的最强“方法演员”方法解决了86%的谜题。我们还测试了OpenAI专为复杂推理任务设计的新模型 o1-preview。当被要求一次性解决谜题时，o1-preview 在我们的数据集中解决了79%的Connections谜题，而当允许通过多次API调用逐步构建谜题解决方案时，o1-preview 解决了100%的谜题。结合“方法演员”提示架构，o1-preview 完美解决的谜题百分比从76%提高到87%。

[NLP-4] Quantitative Assessment of Intersectional Empathetic Bias and Understanding

【速读】： 该论文试图解决当前基于松散定义的共情（empathy）操作化对数据集质量、模型鲁棒性和评估可靠性产生的负面影响。解决方案的关键在于提出一个基于共情心理学起源的操作化评估框架。该框架通过控制生成包含不同社会偏见的提示（prompts）来测量大型语言模型（LLMs）对这些提示的响应差异，从而评估共情和情感极性（emotional valence）。通过这种方式，确保提示数据集中构造的高理论效度，并使得高质量翻译，特别是对目前缺乏共情或偏见评估方法的语言（如斯拉夫语系），变得更加可行。实验结果显示，尽管初始评估样本的差异较小，模型在捕捉提示中微妙变化时表现出显著的推理链变化，这为未来构建评估样本和统计方法测量结果提供了基础。

链接: https://arxiv.org/abs/2411.05777
作者: Vojtech Formanek,Ondrej Sotolar
关键词-EN: growing amount, amount of literature, literature critiques, critiques the current, current operationalizations
类目: Computation and Language (cs.CL); Artificial Intelligence (cs.AI); Human-Computer Interaction (cs.HC)
备注:

点击查看摘要

Abstract:A growing amount of literature critiques the current operationalizations of empathy based on loose definitions of the construct. Such definitions negatively affect dataset quality, model robustness, and evaluation reliability. We propose an empathy evaluation framework that operationalizes empathy close to its psychological origins. The framework measures the variance in responses of LLMs to prompts using existing metrics for empathy and emotional valence. The variance is introduced through the controlled generation of the prompts by varying social biases affecting context understanding, thus impacting empathetic understanding. The control over generation ensures high theoretical validity of the constructs in the prompt dataset. Also, it makes high-quality translation, especially into languages that currently have little-to-no way of evaluating empathy or bias, such as the Slavonic family, more manageable. Using chosen LLMs and various prompt types, we demonstrate the empathy evaluation with the framework, including multiple-choice answers and free generation. The variance in our initial evaluation sample is small and we were unable to measure convincing differences between the empathetic understanding in contexts given by different social groups. However, the results are promising because the models showed significant alterations their reasoning chains needed to capture the relatively subtle changes in the prompts. This provides the basis for future research into the construction of the evaluation sample and statistical methods for measuring the results.
摘要：越来越多的文献批评当前基于对同理心概念松散定义的操作化方法。这些定义对数据集质量、模型鲁棒性和评估可靠性产生了负面影响。我们提出了一种同理心评估框架，该框架将同理心操作化接近其心理学根源。该框架通过使用现有的同理心和情感极性指标，测量大语言模型对提示的响应变化。通过控制生成提示时影响上下文理解的社会偏差，从而影响同理心的理解，引入了响应的变化。对生成的控制确保了提示数据集中构念的高理论有效性。此外，它使得高质量的翻译，特别是对目前几乎没有评估同理心或偏差方法的语言，如斯拉夫语系，变得更加可行。我们使用选定的大语言模型和各种提示类型，展示了该框架的同理心评估，包括多项选择答案和自由生成。在我们初步评估样本中，响应的变化较小，我们无法测量不同社会群体提供的上下文中同理心理解的说服性差异。然而，结果是令人鼓舞的，因为模型在捕捉提示中相对细微的变化时，其推理链显示了显著的改变。这为未来研究评估样本的构建和测量结果的统计方法提供了基础。

[NLP-5] Fact or Fiction? Can LLM s be Reliable Annotators for Political Truths? NEURIPS2024

【速读】： 该论文试图解决政治虚假信息对民主进程的挑战，特别是传统事实核查方法在可扩展性和标注者偏见方面的问题。解决方案的关键在于利用最先进的大型语言模型 (LLMs) 作为可靠的标注工具，通过生成标注来识别新闻文章中的政治事实性。研究通过开源LLMs创建了一个政治多样性的数据集，并使用LLM生成的标注进行偏见标记，这些标注经过人类专家验证，并由基于LLM的评判系统进一步评估其准确性和可靠性。这种方法提供了一种可扩展且稳健的替代传统事实核查的方案，增强了媒体透明度和公众信任。

链接: https://arxiv.org/abs/2411.05775
作者: Veronica Chatrath,Marcelo Lotif,Shaina Raza
关键词-EN: misinformation poses significant, poses significant challenges, Political misinformation poses, shaping public opinion, democratic processes
类目: Computation and Language (cs.CL); Artificial Intelligence (cs.AI)
备注: Accepted at Socially Responsible Language Modelling Research (SoLaR) Workshop at NeurIPS 2024

点击查看摘要

Abstract:Political misinformation poses significant challenges to democratic processes, shaping public opinion and trust in media. Manual fact-checking methods face issues of scalability and annotator bias, while machine learning models require large, costly labelled datasets. This study investigates the use of state-of-the-art large language models (LLMs) as reliable annotators for detecting political factuality in news articles. Using open-source LLMs, we create a politically diverse dataset, labelled for bias through LLM-generated annotations. These annotations are validated by human experts and further evaluated by LLM-based judges to assess the accuracy and reliability of the annotations. Our approach offers a scalable and robust alternative to traditional fact-checking, enhancing transparency and public trust in media.
摘要：政治虚假信息对民主进程构成了重大挑战，影响公众舆论和对媒体的信任。人工事实核查方法面临可扩展性和标注者偏见的问题，而机器学习模型则需要大量且昂贵的标注数据集。本研究探讨了使用最先进的大语言模型 (LLM) 作为检测新闻文章中政治事实性的可靠标注工具。我们利用开源的 LLM 创建了一个政治多样性的数据集，并通过 LLM 生成的标注进行偏见标记。这些标注由人类专家验证，并进一步由基于 LLM 的评判者评估，以确定标注的准确性和可靠性。我们的方法为传统事实核查提供了一种可扩展且稳健的替代方案，增强了媒体透明度和公众信任。

[NLP-6] FinDVer: Explainable Claim Verification over Long and Hybrid-Content Financial Documents EMNLP2024

Abstract:We introduce FinDVer, a comprehensive benchmark specifically designed to evaluate the explainable claim verification capabilities of LLMs in the context of understanding and analyzing long, hybrid-content financial documents. We further provide in-depth analysis on long-context and RAG setting, Chain-of-Thought reasoning, and model reasoning errors, offering insights to drive future advancements. [NLP-7] Multi-hop Evidence Pursuit Meets the Web: Team Papelo at FEVER 2024 EMNLP2024

【速读】： 该论文试图解决网络上的虚假信息与事实的区分问题，通过结合大型语言模型（LLMs）的推理能力和现代搜索引擎的检索能力，自动化并可解释地验证声明。解决方案的关键在于采用多跳证据追求策略，该策略通过序列到序列模型生成初始问题，搜索并形成答案，然后使用LLM迭代生成后续问题以追求缺失的证据。这种方法相较于一次性生成所有问题的策略，在标签准确性和AVeriTeC评分上均有显著提升。

链接: https://arxiv.org/abs/2411.05762
作者: Christopher Malon
关键词-EN: Separating disinformation, powers of humans, disinformation from fact, web has long, long challenged
类目: Computation and Language (cs.CL)
备注: To appear in the Seventh FEVER Workshop at EMNLP 2024

点击查看摘要

Abstract:Separating disinformation from fact on the web has long challenged both the search and the reasoning powers of humans. We show that the reasoning power of large language models (LLMs) and the retrieval power of modern search engines can be combined to automate this process and explainably verify claims. We integrate LLMs and search under a multi-hop evidence pursuit strategy. This strategy generates an initial question based on an input claim using a sequence to sequence model, searches and formulates an answer to the question, and iteratively generates follow-up questions to pursue the evidence that is missing using an LLM. We demonstrate our system on the FEVER 2024 (AVeriTeC) shared task. Compared to a strategy of generating all the questions at once, our method obtains .045 higher label accuracy and .155 higher AVeriTeC score (evaluating the adequacy of the evidence). Through ablations, we show the importance of various design choices, such as the question generation method, medium-sized context, reasoning with one document at a time, adding metadata, paraphrasing, reducing the problem to two classes, and reconsidering the final verdict. Our submitted system achieves .510 AVeriTeC score on the dev set and .477 AVeriTeC score on the test set.
摘要：在网络上区分虚假信息与事实长期以来一直是人类搜索和推理能力的挑战。我们展示了如何将大语言模型 (LLMs) 的推理能力和现代搜索引擎的检索能力结合起来，自动化这一过程并可解释地验证声明。我们将 LLMs 和搜索引擎集成在一个多跳证据追踪策略下。该策略首先基于输入声明使用序列到序列模型生成一个初始问题，然后搜索并形成对该问题的答案，并迭代生成后续问题以追踪使用 LLM 缺失的证据。我们在 FEVER 2024 (AVeriTeC) 共享任务中展示了我们的系统。与一次性生成所有问题的策略相比，我们的方法在标签准确性上提高了 0.045，在 AVeriTeC 评分（评估证据的充分性）上提高了 0.155。通过消融实验，我们展示了各种设计选择的重要性，如问题生成方法、中等大小的上下文、一次推理一个文档、添加元数据、改写、将问题简化为两类以及重新考虑最终裁决。我们提交的系统在开发集上达到了 0.510 的 AVeriTeC 评分，在测试集上达到了 0.477 的 AVeriTeC 评分。

Abstract:We present VLMnav, an embodied framework to transform a Vision-Language Model (VLM) into an end-to-end navigation policy. [NLP-9] FisherMask: Enhancing Neural Network Labeling Efficiency in Image Classification Using Fisher Information

【速读】： 该论文试图解决深度学习模型在训练过程中对大量标注数据的依赖问题。解决方案的关键是提出了一种基于Fisher信息（Fisher information）的主动学习（Active Learning, AL）方法，称为FisherMask。FisherMask通过利用Fisher信息值来识别和遮蔽网络中的关键参数，从而在主动学习过程中选择最具影响力的样本进行训练。这种方法不仅减少了模型对大量标注数据的依赖，还通过Fisher信息的统计特性提供了对模型行为和性能特征的深入理解，从而显著提高了标注效率和模型性能，特别是在数据不平衡的情况下。

Abstract:Deep learning (DL) models are popular across various domains due to their remarkable performance and efficiency. However, their effectiveness relies heavily on large amounts of labeled data, which are often time-consuming and labor-intensive to generate manually. To overcome this challenge, it is essential to develop strategies that reduce reliance on extensive labeled data while preserving model performance. In this paper, we propose FisherMask, a Fisher information-based active learning (AL) approach that identifies key network parameters by masking them based on their Fisher information values. FisherMask enhances batch AL by using Fisher information to select the most critical parameters, allowing the identification of the most impactful samples during AL training. Moreover, Fisher information possesses favorable statistical properties, offering valuable insights into model behavior and providing a better understanding of the performance characteristics within the AL pipeline. Our extensive experiments demonstrate that FisherMask significantly outperforms state-of-the-art methods on diverse datasets, including CIFAR-10 and FashionMNIST, especially under imbalanced settings. These improvements lead to substantial gains in labeling efficiency. Hence serving as an effective tool to measure the sensitivity of model parameters to data samples. Our code is available on \urlthis https URL.
摘要：深度学习 (Deep Learning, DL) 模型因其卓越的性能和效率而在各个领域广受欢迎。然而，其有效性在很大程度上依赖于大量的标注数据，这些数据通常需要耗费大量时间和人力来手动生成。为了克服这一挑战，开发减少对大量标注数据依赖的策略，同时保持模型性能，显得尤为重要。本文提出了一种基于 Fisher 信息 (Fisher information) 的主动学习 (Active Learning, AL) 方法，称为 FisherMask。该方法通过根据 Fisher 信息值对网络参数进行掩码处理，识别关键网络参数。FisherMask 通过利用 Fisher 信息来选择最关键的参数，从而在主动学习训练过程中识别出最具影响力的样本，增强了批量主动学习的效果。此外，Fisher 信息具有良好的统计特性，能够深入洞察模型行为，并更好地理解主动学习流程中的性能特征。我们的广泛实验表明，FisherMask 在包括 CIFAR-10 和 FashionMNIST 在内的多种数据集上显著优于最先进的方法，特别是在不平衡设置下。这些改进带来了标注效率的显著提升，从而成为衡量模型参数对数据样本敏感性的有效工具。我们的代码可在 \urlthis https URL 获取。

[NLP-10] Aioli: A Unified Optimization Framework for Language Model Data Mixing

【速读】： 该论文试图解决的问题是如何在训练语言模型时，有效地确定数据组（如法律、代码、数学等）的最佳混合比例，以优化模型性能。解决方案的关键在于统一现有方法到一个标准的优化框架中，揭示了现有方法在设定混合比例时存在的参数化误差问题，并提出了一个新的在线方法Aioli。Aioli通过在整个训练过程中动态估计混合比例参数，从而更准确地调整数据组的比例，显著提升了模型在多个数据集上的测试困惑度（test perplexity）表现。

链接: https://arxiv.org/abs/2411.05735
作者: Mayee F. Chen,Michael Y. Hu,Nicholas Lourie,Kyunghyun Cho,Christopher Ré
关键词-EN: Language model performance, Language model, depends on identifying, identifying the optimal, model performance depends
类目: Machine Learning (cs.LG); Artificial Intelligence (cs.AI); Computation and Language (cs.CL); Machine Learning (stat.ML)
备注:

点击查看摘要

Abstract:Language model performance depends on identifying the optimal mixture of data groups to train on (e.g., law, code, math). Prior work has proposed a diverse set of methods to efficiently learn mixture proportions, ranging from fitting regression models over training runs to dynamically updating proportions throughout training. Surprisingly, we find that no existing method consistently outperforms a simple stratified sampling baseline in terms of average test perplexity per group. In this paper, we study the cause of this inconsistency by unifying existing methods into a standard optimization framework. We show that all methods set proportions to minimize total loss, subject to a method-specific mixing law – an assumption on how loss is a function of mixture proportions. We find that existing parameterizations of mixing laws can express the true loss-proportion relationship empirically, but the methods themselves often set the mixing law parameters inaccurately, resulting in poor and inconsistent performance. Finally, we leverage the insights from our framework to derive a new online method named Aioli, which directly estimates the mixing law parameters throughout training and uses them to dynamically adjust proportions. Empirically, Aioli outperforms stratified sampling on 6 out of 6 datasets by an average of 0.28 test perplexity points, whereas existing methods fail to consistently beat stratified sampling, doing up to 6.9 points worse. Moreover, in a practical setting where proportions are learned on shorter runs due to computational constraints, Aioli can dynamically adjust these proportions over the full training run, consistently improving performance over existing methods by up to 12.01 test perplexity points.
摘要：语言模型的性能取决于识别出用于训练的最佳数据组混合比例（例如，法律、代码、数学）。先前的工作提出了多种方法来高效地学习混合比例，从在训练过程中拟合回归模型到在整个训练过程中动态更新比例。令人惊讶的是，我们发现现有方法在各组的平均测试困惑度方面均未能持续超越简单的分层抽样基线。本文通过将现有方法统一到一个标准的优化框架中，研究了这种不一致性的原因。我们表明，所有方法都设定比例以最小化总损失，但受限于特定方法的混合定律——即关于损失如何作为混合比例函数的假设。我们发现，现有混合定律的参数化方法在经验上可以表达真实的损失-比例关系，但这些方法本身往往设定混合定律参数不准确，导致性能不佳且不一致。最后，我们利用框架中的见解推导出一种名为Aioli的新在线方法，该方法在整个训练过程中直接估计混合定律参数，并使用它们动态调整比例。在实验中，Aioli在6个数据集中的6个上均优于分层抽样，平均降低了0.28个测试困惑度点，而现有方法未能持续超越分层抽样，最差时高达6.9个点。此外，在实际应用中，由于计算限制，比例在较短的运行中学习，Aioli可以在整个训练过程中动态调整这些比例，持续提高性能，最多可比现有方法提升12.01个测试困惑度点。

[NLP-11] Image2Text2Image: A Novel Framework for Label-Free Evaluation of Image-to-Text Generation with Text-to-Image Diffusion Models

【速读】： 该论文试图解决自动生成图像描述质量评估的复杂性问题，现有的自动化评估指标（如BLEU, ROUGE, METEOR, CIDEr）与人类判断之间的相关性较弱。论文提出的解决方案之关键是引入了一种名为Image2Text2Image的新评估框架，该框架利用扩散模型（如Stable Diffusion或DALL-E）进行文本到图像的生成。具体步骤包括：首先使用待评估的图像描述模型生成图像的文本描述，然后利用扩散模型根据生成的描述创建新图像，最后通过比较原始图像与生成图像的特征相似度来评估描述的准确性。该方法不依赖于人工标注的参考描述，从而提供了一种有效的自动化评估工具。

链接: https://arxiv.org/abs/2411.05706
作者: Jia-Hong Huang,Hongyi Zhu,Yixian Shen,Stevan Rudinac,Evangelos Kanoulas
关键词-EN: Evaluating the quality, requires metrics capturing, capturing various dimensions, quality of automatically, complex task
类目: Computer Vision and Pattern Recognition (cs.CV); Computation and Language (cs.CL)
备注: arXiv admin note: substantial text overlap with arXiv:2408.01723

点击查看摘要

Abstract:Evaluating the quality of automatically generated image descriptions is a complex task that requires metrics capturing various dimensions, such as grammaticality, coverage, accuracy, and truthfulness. Although human evaluation provides valuable insights, its cost and time-consuming nature pose limitations. Existing automated metrics like BLEU, ROUGE, METEOR, and CIDEr attempt to fill this gap, but they often exhibit weak correlations with human judgment. To address this challenge, we propose a novel evaluation framework called Image2Text2Image, which leverages diffusion models, such as Stable Diffusion or DALL-E, for text-to-image generation. In the Image2Text2Image framework, an input image is first processed by a selected image captioning model, chosen for evaluation, to generate a textual description. Using this generated description, a diffusion model then creates a new image. By comparing features extracted from the original and generated images, we measure their similarity using a designated similarity metric. A high similarity score suggests that the model has produced a faithful textual description, while a low score highlights discrepancies, revealing potential weaknesses in the model’s performance. Notably, our framework does not rely on human-annotated reference captions, making it a valuable tool for assessing image captioning models. Extensive experiments and human evaluations validate the efficacy of our proposed Image2Text2Image evaluation framework. The code and dataset will be published to support further research in the community.
摘要：评估自动生成图像描述的质量是一项复杂的任务，需要捕捉语法性、覆盖率、准确性和真实性等多个维度的指标。尽管人工评估提供了宝贵的见解，但其成本高昂且耗时，存在一定的局限性。现有的自动化指标如 BLEU、ROUGE、METEOR 和 CIDEr 试图填补这一空白，但它们往往与人类判断的相关性较弱。为应对这一挑战，我们提出了一种名为 Image2Text2Image 的新型评估框架，该框架利用扩散模型（如 Stable Diffusion 或 DALL-E）进行文本到图像的生成。在 Image2Text2Image 框架中，输入图像首先由选定的图像描述生成模型（用于评估）处理，生成一段文本描述。然后，利用生成的描述，扩散模型创建一张新图像。通过比较从原始图像和生成图像中提取的特征，我们使用指定的相似度度量来衡量它们的相似度。高相似度分数表明模型生成了忠实的文本描述，而低分数则突显了差异，揭示了模型性能的潜在弱点。值得注意的是，我们的框架不依赖于人工标注的参考描述，使其成为评估图像描述生成模型的宝贵工具。广泛的实验和人工评估验证了我们提出的 Image2Text2Image 评估框架的有效性。代码和数据集将发布，以支持社区的进一步研究。

[NLP-12] Asterisk*: Keep it Simple

【速读】： 该论文试图解决在生成文本嵌入时，如何在保持模型性能的同时最小化计算和内存需求的问题。解决方案的关键在于采用了一种极简主义的架构设计，即Asterisk模型，该模型基于GPT架构，仅包含两层、两个注意力头和256维嵌入维度。通过从更大的预训练模型中应用知识蒸馏（knowledge distillation），研究者在模型大小与性能之间进行了权衡，从而在减少计算和内存需求的同时，仍能保持一定的分类任务性能。实验结果表明，该模型在零样本分类任务中表现出中等性能，并且在特定分类任务上，通过额外配置，其性能可以接近甚至超越更大架构的模型。

链接: https://arxiv.org/abs/2411.05691
作者: Andrew Semenov
关键词-EN: paper describes Asterisk, describes Asterisk, generating text embeddings, compact GPT-based model, paper describes
类目: Computation and Language (cs.CL); Artificial Intelligence (cs.AI)
备注:

点击查看摘要

Abstract:This paper describes Asterisk, a compact GPT-based model for generating text embeddings. The model uses a minimalist architecture with two layers, two attention heads, and 256 embedding dimensions. By applying knowledge distillation from larger pretrained models, we explore the trade-offs between model size and performance while minimizing computational and memory requirements. The model is primarily evaluated and optimized for classification tasks, with experimental results showing its moderate performance in zero-shot classification across various downstream applications. With additional configuration, the model performance can approach or even surpass that of larger architectures on specific classification tasks.
摘要：本文介绍了 Asterisk，一个基于 GPT 的紧凑型模型，用于生成文本嵌入。该模型采用极简架构，包含两层、两个注意力头和 256 维嵌入维度。通过从更大的预训练模型中应用知识蒸馏，我们在最小化计算和内存需求的同时，探讨了模型大小与性能之间的权衡。该模型主要针对分类任务进行评估和优化，实验结果显示其在各种下游应用中的零样本分类任务中表现出中等性能。通过额外配置，模型在特定分类任务上的性能可以接近甚至超越更大架构的性能。

[NLP-13] Unmasking the Limits of Large Language Models : A Systematic Evaluation of Masked Text Processing Ability through MskQA and MskCal

【速读】： 该论文旨在揭示大型语言模型（Large Language Models, LLMs）在处理掩码文本时的局限性，并提出了两个新的任务：MskQA（用于评估掩码问答数据集上的推理能力）和MskCal（用于评估掩码算术数据集上的数值推理能力）。研究的关键在于通过对比不同掩码策略（如“完全掩码”和“部分保留”）对模型性能的影响，发现LLMs在处理掩码文本时严重依赖于表面层次的模式和语义线索。具体来说，当语义线索完全缺失时（完全掩码），模型的性能显著下降，而当部分语义信息保留时（部分保留），性能有所提升。此外，研究还发现GPT-4o在处理掩码文本的数值推理任务上表现优于4o-mini，这表明语义线索在LLMs的推理过程中起着至关重要的作用。该研究为深入理解LLMs的能力和局限性提供了新的视角，并强调了开发更鲁棒的评估方法以准确评估其真正理解能力的重要性。

链接: https://arxiv.org/abs/2411.05665
作者: Fuka Matsuzaki,Haru-Tada Sato
关键词-EN: Large Language Models, Language Models, Large Language, paper sheds light, paper sheds
类目: Computation and Language (cs.CL)
备注: 16 pages

点击查看摘要

Abstract:This paper sheds light on the limitations of Large Language Models (LLMs) by rigorously evaluating their ability to process masked text. We introduce two novel tasks: MskQA, measuring reasoning on masked question-answering datasets like RealtimeQA, and MskCal, assessing numerical reasoning on masked arithmetic this http URL GPT-4o and 4o-mini reveals that while LLMs exhibit some resilience to masked text, their performance is highly contingent on masking rates and semantic cues. Specifically, “solid masking,” where semantic clues are entirely absent, leads to a significant performance drop compared to “partial lifting,” where some semantic information is retained, indicating LLMs’ reliance on surface-level patterns. Interestingly, GPT-4o consistently outperforms 4o-mini, particularly in MskCal, demonstrating a greater ability to handle numerical reasoning with masked text. This underscores the crucial role of semantic cues in the reasoning process of LLMs. Our study illuminates the interplay between background knowledge and reasoning ability in masked text processing, paving the way for a deeper understanding of LLM capabilities and limitations, and highlighting the need for more robust evaluation methods to accurately assess their true comprehension abilities.
摘要：本文通过严格评估大语言模型 (LLM) 处理掩码文本的能力，揭示了其局限性。我们引入了两个新任务：MskQA，用于测量在掩码问答数据集（如 RealtimeQA）上的推理能力；MskCal，用于评估在掩码算术任务上的数值推理能力。通过对 GPT-4o 和 4o-mini 的实验，我们发现尽管 LLM 对掩码文本表现出一定的韧性，但其性能高度依赖于掩码率和语义线索。具体而言，“完全掩码”（即语义线索完全缺失）相较于“部分保留”（即保留部分语义信息），会导致显著的性能下降，这表明 LLM 依赖于表面层次的模式。有趣的是，GPT-4o 在 MskCal 任务中始终优于 4o-mini，特别是在处理掩码文本的数值推理方面，显示出更强的能力。这突显了语义线索在 LLM 推理过程中的关键作用。我们的研究揭示了背景知识与推理能力在掩码文本处理中的相互作用，为进一步深入理解 LLM 的能力和局限性铺平了道路，并强调了需要更强大的评估方法来准确评估其真正的理解能力。

Abstract:Large Language Models (LLMs), with gradually improving reading comprehension and reasoning capabilities, are being applied to a range of complex language tasks, including the automatic generation of language data for various purposes. However, research on applying LLMs for automatic data generation in low-resource languages like Vietnamese is still underdeveloped and lacks comprehensive evaluation. In this paper, we explore the use of LLMs for automatic data generation for the Vietnamese fact-checking task, which faces significant data limitations. Specifically, we focus on fact-checking data where claims are synthesized from multiple evidence sentences to assess the information synthesis capabilities of LLMs. We develop an automatic data construction process using simple prompt techniques on LLMs and explore several methods to improve the quality of the generated data. To evaluate the quality of the data generated by LLMs, we conduct both manual quality assessments and performance evaluations using language models. Abstract:This study examines how fake news affects social media users across a range of age groups and how machine learning (ML) and artificial intelligence (AI) can help reduce the spread of false information. Abstract:Wikipedia’s perceived high quality and broad language coverage have established it as a fundamental resource in multilingual NLP. In the context of low-resource languages, however, these quality assumptions are increasingly being scrutinised. This paper critically examines the data quality of Wikipedia in a non-English setting by subjecting it to various quality filtering techniques, revealing widespread issues such as a high percentage of one-line articles and duplicate articles. We evaluate the downstream impact of quality filtering on Wikipedia and find that data quality pruning is an effective means for resource-efficient training without hurting performance, especially for low-resource languages. 摘要：维基百科因其被认为的高质量和广泛的语言覆盖范围，已成为多语言自然语言处理（NLP）中的基础资源。然而，在低资源语言的背景下，这些质量假设正日益受到质疑。本文通过将维基百科置于非英语环境中，采用多种质量过滤技术对其进行批判性分析，揭示了广泛存在的问题，如高比例的单行文章和重复文章。我们评估了质量过滤对维基百科下游任务的影响，发现数据质量修剪是一种有效的资源高效训练手段，且不会损害性能，尤其适用于低资源语言。此外，我们主张从寻求数据质量的通用定义转向更具语言和任务特异性的定义。最终，我们希望本研究能为在多语言环境中使用维基百科进行预训练提供指导。

[NLP-20] An Early FIRST Reproduction and Improvements to Single-Token Decoding for Fast Listwise Reranking

【速读】： 该论文试图解决大型语言模型（LLMs）在作为列表重排序器时的高计算需求问题，并提出了一种名为FIRST的新方法。解决方案的关键在于将学习排序目标（learning-to-rank objective）与仅利用生成的第一个token的logits相结合，从而显著减少推理延迟。通过在TREC Deep Learning数据集（DL19-22）上的扩展评估，验证了FIRST在不同领域的鲁棒性，并展示了其在不同骨干模型上的有效性提升。实验结果表明，使用单个token的logits进行快速重排序不会牺牲跨领域的重排序质量，同时实现了21%-42%的延迟减少。此外，研究还探讨了语言模型预训练对后续FIRST目标微调的影响，提出了关于预训练可能阻碍微调效果的疑问。

链接: https://arxiv.org/abs/2411.05508
作者: Zijian Chen,Ronak Pradeep,Jimmy Lin
关键词-EN: traditional LLM rerankers, Recent advances, high computational demands, computational demands remain, LLM rerankers
类目: Information Retrieval (cs.IR); Computation and Language (cs.CL)
备注:

点击查看摘要

Abstract:Recent advances have demonstrated that large language models (LLMs) excel as listwise rerankers, but their high computational demands remain a barrier to widespread adoption. Further, the traditional language modeling (LM) objective is not ideally suited for reranking tasks. FIRST is a novel approach that addresses these challenges by integrating a learning-to-rank objective and leveraging the logits of only the first generated token, thereby significantly reducing inference latency compared to traditional LLM rerankers. In this study, we extend the evaluation of FIRST to the TREC Deep Learning datasets (DL19-22), validating its robustness across diverse domains. We investigate the influence of different first-stage retrievers on FIRST rerankers, observing diminishing returns and patterns consistent with traditional LLM rerankers. Through applying the FIRST objective to a broader range of backbone models, we achieve effectiveness surpassing the original implementation. Our experiments confirm that fast reranking with single-token logits does not compromise out-of-domain reranking quality. To better quantify the computational savings in the original study, we measure and compare latency to find a 21%-42% gain across various models and benchmarks. Moreover, while LM training implicitly improves zero-shot single-token reranking, our experiments also raise questions about whether LM pre-training may hinder subsequent fine-tuning with the FIRST objective. These findings pave the way for more efficient and effective listwise reranking in future applications.
摘要：近期的进展表明，大语言模型 (LLM) 在作为列表式重排序器方面表现出色，但其高计算需求仍然是广泛应用的障碍。此外，传统的语言建模 (LM) 目标并不完全适合重排序任务。FIRST 是一种新颖的方法，通过整合学习排序目标并利用仅第一个生成的 Token 的 Logits，显著减少了与传统 LLM 重排序器相比的推理延迟。在本研究中，我们将 FIRST 的评估扩展到 TREC 深度学习数据集 (DL19-22)，验证了其在不同领域中的稳健性。我们探讨了不同第一阶段检索器对 FIRST 重排序器的影响，观察到收益递减和与传统 LLM 重排序器一致的模式。通过将 FIRST 目标应用于更广泛的主干模型，我们实现了超越原始实现的效果。我们的实验证实，使用单 Token Logits 进行快速重排序不会影响域外重排序的质量。为了更好地量化原始研究中的计算节省，我们测量并比较了延迟，发现在各种模型和基准测试中获得了 21%-42% 的提升。此外，尽管 LM 训练隐含地改进了零样本单 Token 重排序，但我们的实验也提出了关于 LM 预训练是否可能阻碍后续使用 FIRST 目标进行微调的问题。这些发现为未来应用中更高效和有效的列表式重排序铺平了道路。

[NLP-21] LBPE: Long-token-first Tokenization to Improve Large Language Models

【速读】： 该论文试图解决在大语言模型 (Large Language Models, LLMs) 中使用字节对编码 (Byte Pair Encoding, BPE) 时，由于长词元 (long tokens) 在数据集中出现频率较低，导致学习不平衡的问题。解决方案的关键是提出了一种新的编码方法，称为长词元优先编码 (Long-token Byte Pair Encoding, LBPE)。LBPE 在编码过程中优先考虑长词元，根据词元长度的倒序而非词汇表中的顺序生成词元，从而平衡长短词元的频率差异，缓解学习不平衡问题。实验结果表明，LBPE 在多种语言建模任务中均优于传统的 BPE，证明了其有效性。

链接: https://arxiv.org/abs/2411.05504
作者: Haoran Lian,Yizhe Xiong,Zijia Lin,Jianwei Niu,Shasha Mo,Hui Chen,Peng Liu,Guiguang Ding
关键词-EN: Byte Pair Encoding, Large Language Models, Byte Pair, facilitates robust handling, Pair Encoding
类目: Computation and Language (cs.CL)
备注: arXiv admin note: text overlap with arXiv:2404.17808

点击查看摘要

Abstract:The prevalent use of Byte Pair Encoding (BPE) in Large Language Models (LLMs) facilitates robust handling of subword units and avoids issues of out-of-vocabulary words. Despite its success, a critical challenge persists: long tokens, rich in semantic information, have fewer occurrences in tokenized datasets compared to short tokens, which can result in imbalanced learning issue across different tokens. To address that, we propose LBPE, which prioritizes long tokens during the encoding process. LBPE generates tokens according to their reverse ranks of token length rather than their ranks in the vocabulary, granting longer tokens higher priority during the encoding process. Consequently, LBPE smooths the frequency differences between short and long tokens, and thus mitigates the learning imbalance. Extensive experiments across diverse language modeling tasks demonstrate that LBPE consistently outperforms the original BPE, well demonstrating its effectiveness.
摘要：大语言模型 (LLM) 中广泛使用的字节对编码 (Byte Pair Encoding, BPE) 有助于稳健地处理子词单元，并避免词汇外词的问题。尽管取得了成功，但一个关键挑战依然存在：富含语义信息的长 Token 在 Token 化数据集中的出现频率远低于短 Token，这可能导致不同 Token 之间的学习不平衡问题。为解决这一问题，我们提出了 LBPE，该方法在编码过程中优先考虑长 Token。LBPE 根据 Token 长度的倒序而非词汇表中的顺序生成 Token，从而在编码过程中赋予长 Token 更高的优先级。因此，LBPE 平滑了短 Token 和长 Token 之间的频率差异，从而缓解了学习不平衡问题。在多种语言建模任务上的广泛实验表明，LBPE 始终优于原始的 BPE，充分展示了其有效性。

Abstract:Large language models (LLMs) have excelled in numerous benchmarks, advancing AI applications in both linguistic and non-linguistic tasks. However, this has primarily benefited well-resourced languages, leaving less-resourced ones (LRLs) at a disadvantage. In this paper, we highlight the current state of the NLP field in the specific LRL: kyrgyz tili. Human evaluation, including annotated datasets created by native speakers, remains an irreplaceable component of reliable NLP performance, especially for LRLs where automatic evaluations can fall short. In recent assessments of the resources for Turkic languages, Kyrgyz is labeled with the status ‘Scraping By’, a severely under-resourced language spoken by millions. This is concerning given the growing importance of the language, not only in Kyrgyzstan but also among diaspora communities where it holds no official status. We review prior efforts in the field, noting that many of the publicly available resources have only recently been developed, with few exceptions beyond dictionaries (the processed data used for the analysis is presented at this https URL). While recent papers have made some headway, much more remains to be done. Despite interest and support from both business and government sectors in the Kyrgyz Republic, the situation for Kyrgyz language resources remains challenging. We stress the importance of community-driven efforts to build these resources, ensuring the future advancement sustainability. We then share our view of the most pressing challenges in Kyrgyz NLP. Finally, we propose a roadmap for future development in terms of research topics and language resources. 摘要：大语言模型（LLMs）在众多基准测试中表现优异，推动了人工智能在语言和非语言任务中的应用。然而，这一进展主要惠及资源丰富的语言，使得资源匮乏语言（LRLs）处于劣势。本文重点介绍了吉尔吉斯语这一特定资源匮乏语言（LRL）在自然语言处理（NLP）领域的现状。人类评估，包括由母语者创建的标注数据集，仍然是可靠NLP性能中不可替代的组成部分，尤其是在自动评估可能不足的资源匮乏语言中。在最近对突厥语系语言资源的评估中，吉尔吉斯语被标注为“勉强维持”状态，这是一种严重资源匮乏的语言，却有数百万人使用。考虑到该语言不仅在吉尔吉斯斯坦，而且在无官方地位的侨民社区中日益重要，这一情况令人担忧。我们回顾了该领域的先前努力，注意到许多公开资源仅在最近才开发出来，除了词典外几乎没有例外（用于分析的处理数据在此https URL中提供）。尽管最近的一些论文取得了一些进展，但仍有许多工作需要完成。尽管吉尔吉斯共和国的商业和政府部门对此表现出兴趣和支持，但吉尔吉斯语资源的现状仍然充满挑战。我们强调了社区驱动努力构建这些资源的重要性，以确保未来的可持续发展。随后，我们分享了在吉尔吉斯语NLP领域中最紧迫的挑战的看法。最后，我们提出了未来发展的路线图，包括研究课题和语言资源。

[NLP-23] EUREKHA: Enhancing User Representation for Key Hackers Identification in Underground Forums

【速读】： 该论文试图解决在地下论坛中识别关键黑客（key hackers）的问题。解决方案的关键在于提出了一种名为EUREKHA的新方法，通过将每个用户建模为文本序列，并利用大型语言模型（LLM）进行领域特定适应，提取特征后输入图神经网络（GNN）以建模用户结构关系，从而显著提高识别准确性。此外，使用BERTopic进行个性化主题提取，优化文本表示的选择，进一步提升了模型的性能。实验结果表明，EUREKHA在识别关键黑客方面优于现有最先进的方法，准确率和F1-score分别提高了约6%和10%。

链接: https://arxiv.org/abs/2411.05479
作者: Abdoul Nasser Hassane Amadou,Anas Motii,Saida Elouardi,EL Houcine Bergou
关键词-EN: conventional online oversight, Underground forums serve, Underground forums, cybercriminal activities, offering a space
类目: Cryptography and Security (cs.CR); Computation and Language (cs.CL); Social and Information Networks (cs.SI)
备注: Accepted at IEEE Trustcom 2024

点击查看摘要

Abstract:Underground forums serve as hubs for cybercriminal activities, offering a space for anonymity and evasion of conventional online oversight. In these hidden communities, malicious actors collaborate to exchange illicit knowledge, tools, and tactics, driving a range of cyber threats from hacking techniques to the sale of stolen data, malware, and zero-day exploits. Identifying the key instigators (i.e., key hackers), behind these operations is essential but remains a complex challenge. This paper presents a novel method called EUREKHA (Enhancing User Representation for Key Hacker Identification in Underground Forums), designed to identify these key hackers by modeling each user as a textual sequence. This sequence is processed through a large language model (LLM) for domain-specific adaptation, with LLMs acting as feature extractors. These extracted features are then fed into a Graph Neural Network (GNN) to model user structural relationships, significantly improving identification accuracy. Furthermore, we employ BERTopic (Bidirectional Encoder Representations from Transformers Topic Modeling) to extract personalized topics from user-generated content, enabling multiple textual representations per user and optimizing the selection of the most representative sequence. Our study demonstrates that fine-tuned LLMs outperform state-of-the-art methods in identifying key hackers. Additionally, when combined with GNNs, our model achieves significant improvements, resulting in approximately 6% and 10% increases in accuracy and F1-score, respectively, over existing methods. EUREKHA was tested on the Hack-Forums dataset, and we provide open-source access to our code.
摘要：地下论坛作为网络犯罪活动的中心，提供了匿名性和规避传统在线监管的空间。在这些隐蔽的社区中，恶意行为者合作交流非法知识、工具和策略，推动了从黑客技术到被盗数据、恶意软件和零日漏洞销售的多种网络威胁。识别这些操作背后的关键煽动者（即关键黑客）至关重要，但仍是一个复杂的挑战。本文提出了一种名为 EUREKHA（Enhancing User Representation for Key Hacker Identification in Underground Forums）的新方法，通过将每个用户建模为文本序列来识别这些关键黑客。该序列通过大语言模型（LLM）进行领域特定适应处理，LLM 作为特征提取器。提取的特征随后被输入图神经网络（GNN）以建模用户结构关系，显著提高了识别准确性。此外，我们采用 BERTopic（Bidirectional Encoder Representations from Transformers Topic Modeling）从用户生成内容中提取个性化主题，从而实现每个用户的多种文本表示，并优化最具代表性序列的选择。我们的研究表明，经过微调的 LLM 在识别关键黑客方面优于最先进的方法。此外，当与 GNN 结合时，我们的模型实现了显著的改进，准确率和 F1 分数分别比现有方法提高了约 6% 和 10%。EUREKHA 在 Hack-Forums 数据集上进行了测试，并提供了开源代码访问。

[NLP-24] Supporting Automated Fact-checking across Topics: Similarity-driven Gradual Topic Learning for Claim Detection

Abstract:Selecting check-worthy claims for fact-checking is considered a crucial part of expediting the fact-checking process by filtering out and ranking the check-worthy claims for being validated among the impressive amount of claims could be found online. The check-worthy claim detection task, however, becomes more challenging when the model needs to deal with new topics that differ from those seen earlier. In this study, we propose a domain-adaptation framework for check-worthy claims detection across topics for the Arabic language to adopt a new topic, mimicking a real-life scenario of the daily emergence of events worldwide. We propose the Gradual Topic Learning (GTL) model, which builds an ability to learning gradually and emphasizes the check-worthy claims for the target topic during several stages of the learning process. In addition, we introduce the Similarity-driven Gradual Topic Learning (SGTL) model that synthesizes gradual learning with a similarity-based strategy for the target topic. Our experiments demonstrate the effectiveness of our proposed model, showing an overall tendency for improving performance over the state-of-the-art baseline across 11 out of the 14 topics under study.
摘要：选择值得核查的主张进行事实核查是加快事实核查过程的关键部分，通过筛选和排序大量在线主张中值得验证的主张。然而，当模型需要处理与之前所见主题不同的新主题时，值得核查主张的检测任务变得更加具有挑战性。在本研究中，我们为阿拉伯语的跨主题值得核查主张检测提出了一种领域适应框架，以模拟全球每日事件涌现的真实场景来适应新主题。我们提出了渐进主题学习（Gradual Topic Learning, GTL）模型，该模型在学习的多个阶段逐步构建学习能力，并强调目标主题的值得核查主张。此外，我们引入了基于相似性的渐进主题学习（Similarity-driven Gradual Topic Learning, SGTL）模型，该模型将渐进学习与基于相似性的策略相结合，用于目标主题。我们的实验结果表明，所提出的模型具有有效性，显示出在研究的14个主题中，有11个主题的性能优于当前最先进的基线模型。

[NLP-25] WorkflowLLM : Enhancing Workflow Orchestration Capability of Large Language Models

【速读】： 该论文试图解决现有大型语言模型（LLMs）在流程自动化中的工作流编排能力不足的问题。解决方案的关键在于提出了一个以数据为中心的框架WorkflowLLM，通过构建大规模的微调数据集WorkflowBench来增强LLMs在工作流编排中的能力。WorkflowBench包含106,763个样本，涵盖1,503个API，涉及83个应用程序和28个类别。其构建过程包括数据收集、查询扩展和流程生成三个阶段，最终通过WorkflowBench微调Llama-3.1-8B模型，得到WorkflowLlama，实验结果表明WorkflowLlama在复杂工作流编排和泛化性能方面表现出色。

链接: https://arxiv.org/abs/2411.05451
作者: Shengda Fan,Xin Cong,Yuepeng Fu,Zhong Zhang,Shuyan Zhang,Yuanwei Liu,Yesai Wu,Yankai Lin,Zhiyuan Liu,Maosong Sun
关键词-EN: Robotic Process Automation, Agentic Process Automation, process automation, revolutionary paradigm shift, Recent advancements
类目: oftware Engineering (cs.SE); Artificial Intelligence (cs.AI); Computation and Language (cs.CL)
备注:

点击查看摘要

Abstract:Recent advancements in large language models (LLMs) have driven a revolutionary paradigm shift in process automation from Robotic Process Automation to Agentic Process Automation by automating the workflow orchestration procedure based on LLMs. However, existing LLMs (even the advanced OpenAI GPT-4o) are confined to achieving satisfactory capability in workflow orchestration. To address this limitation, we present WorkflowLLM, a data-centric framework elaborately designed to enhance the capability of LLMs in workflow orchestration. It first constructs a large-scale fine-tuning dataset WorkflowBench with 106,763 samples, covering 1,503 APIs from 83 applications across 28 categories. Specifically, the construction process can be divided into three phases: (1) Data Collection: we collect real-world workflow data from Apple Shortcuts and RoutineHub, transcribing them into Python-style code. We further equip them with generated hierarchical thought via ChatGPT. (2) Query Expansion: we prompt ChatGPT to generate more task queries to enrich the diversity and complexity of workflows. (3) Workflow Generation: we leverage an annotator model trained on collected data to generate workflows for synthesized queries. Finally, we merge the synthetic samples that pass quality confirmation with the collected samples to obtain the WorkflowBench. Based on WorkflowBench, we fine-tune Llama-3.1-8B to obtain WorkflowLlama. Our experiments show that WorkflowLlama demonstrates a strong capacity to orchestrate complex workflows, while also achieving notable generalization performance on previously unseen APIs. Additionally, WorkflowBench exhibits robust zero-shot generalization capabilities on an out-of-distribution task planning dataset, T-Eval. Our data and code are available at this https URL.
摘要：近年来，大语言模型（LLMs）的进步推动了从机器人流程自动化到智能体流程自动化的革命性范式转变，通过基于LLMs的自动化工作流编排程序实现。然而，现有的LLMs（即使是先进的OpenAI GPT-4o）在工作流编排方面的能力仍有限。为解决这一局限，我们提出了WorkflowLLM，一个以数据为中心的框架，精心设计以增强LLMs在工作流编排中的能力。首先，我们构建了一个大规模的微调数据集WorkflowBench，包含106,763个样本，涵盖了来自83个应用程序的1,503个API，分布在28个类别中。具体构建过程可分为三个阶段：（1）数据收集：我们从Apple Shortcuts和RoutineHub收集现实世界的工作流数据，并将其转录为Python风格的代码。我们还通过ChatGPT为这些数据生成了层次化的思维结构。（2）查询扩展：我们提示ChatGPT生成更多任务查询，以丰富工作流的多样性和复杂性。（3）工作流生成：我们利用基于收集数据训练的注释模型来生成合成查询的工作流。最后，我们将通过质量确认的合成样本与收集的样本合并，得到WorkflowBench。基于WorkflowBench，我们微调了Llama-3.1-8B以获得WorkflowLlama。我们的实验表明，WorkflowLlama展示了强大的复杂工作流编排能力，同时在先前未见过的API上也表现出显著的泛化性能。此外，WorkflowBench在分布外任务规划数据集T-Eval上展示了稳健的零样本泛化能力。我们的数据和代码可通过此https URL获取。

Abstract:Generating accurate and consistent visual aids is a critical challenge in mathematics education, where visual representations like geometric shapes and functions play a pivotal role in enhancing student comprehension. [NLP-27] Gap-Filling Prompting Enhances Code-Assisted Mathematical Reasoning

【速读】： 该论文试图解决小型语言模型（SLMs）在数学推理任务中由于信息缺失导致的理解困难和计算错误问题。解决方案的关键在于引入了一种名为“Gap-Filling Prompting (GFP)”的新型两步提示策略。第一步是识别问题中的信息缺失（gaps）并提供填充这些缺失的提示，第二步是将这些提示添加到问题中，以生成最终的代码解决方案。通过这种方式，GFP显著提升了SLMs在数学推理任务中的表现。

链接: https://arxiv.org/abs/2411.05407
作者: Mohammad Ghiasvand Mohammadkhani
关键词-EN: high computational demands, large language models, small language models, language models, proprietary restrictions
类目: Computation and Language (cs.CL)
备注:

点击查看摘要

Abstract:Despite the strong performance of large language models (LLMs) in tasks like mathematical reasoning, their practical use is limited by high computational demands and proprietary restrictions. Chain-of-thought (CoT) and program-of-thought (PoT) fine-tuning are common methods to transfer LLM knowledge to small language models (SLMs). However, CoT often leads to calculation errors in SLMs, while PoT has shown more promise. While most PoT-based approaches focus on direct problem-to-code conversion or extracting only the key information from questions and then providing code solution for it, this work emphasizes filling the gaps in the question to clearly illustrate the solution path, which can be challenging for an SLM to understand when such information is not explicitly provided. Therefore, this paper introduces Gap-Filling Prompting (GFP), a novel two-step prompting strategy designed to enhance the problem-solving process for SLMs. The first step identifies these gaps and provides hints for filling them, while the second step adds the hints to the question to generate a final code solution. Experimental results on two benchmark datasets demonstrate that GFP significantly improves the mathematical reasoning abilities of SLMs.
摘要：尽管大语言模型（Large Language Models, LLMs）在数学推理等任务中表现出色，但其实际应用受到高计算需求和专有限制的制约。思维链（Chain-of-thought, CoT）和思维程序（Program-of-thought, PoT）微调是将 LLM 知识转移到小语言模型（Small Language Models, SLMs）的常见方法。然而，CoT 往往导致 SLMs 在计算中出现错误，而 PoT 则显示出更大的潜力。尽管大多数基于 PoT 的方法侧重于直接的问题到代码转换，或仅从问题中提取关键信息并为其提供代码解决方案，但本研究强调填补问题中的空白以清晰地说明解决方案路径，这对于 SLM 来说在信息未明确提供时理解起来具有挑战性。因此，本文引入了空白填充提示（Gap-Filling Prompting, GFP），这是一种新颖的两步提示策略，旨在增强 SLMs 的问题解决过程。第一步识别这些空白并提供填充提示，第二步将提示添加到问题中以生成最终的代码解决方案。在两个基准数据集上的实验结果表明，GFP 显著提升了 SLMs 的数学推理能力。

Abstract:Language models (LMs) are increasingly used as simulacra for people, yet their ability to match the distribution of views of a specific demographic group and be \textitdistributionally aligned remains uncertain. This notion of distributional alignment is complex, as there is significant variation in the types of attributes that are simulated. Prior works have underexplored the role of three critical variables – the question domain, steering method, and distribution expression method – which motivates our contribution of a benchmark explicitly addressing these dimensions. We construct a dataset expanding beyond political values, create human baselines for this task, and evaluate the extent to which an LM can align with a particular group’s opinion distribution to inform design choices of such simulation systems. Our analysis reveals open problems regarding if, and how, LMs can be used to simulate humans, and that LLMs can more accurately describe the opinion distribution than simulate such distributions.
摘要：语言模型（Language Models, LMs）越来越多地被用作人类的模拟体，但其能否匹配特定人群的观点分布并实现分布对齐（distributionally aligned）仍不确定。分布对齐的概念复杂，因为模拟的属性类型存在显著差异。先前的工作在三个关键变量——问题领域（question domain）、引导方法（steering method）和分布表达方法（distribution expression method）——的作用上探索不足，这促使我们贡献了一个明确针对这些维度的基准测试。我们构建了一个超越政治价值观的数据集，为此任务创建了人类基线，并评估了语言模型在多大程度上能够与特定群体的观点分布对齐，以指导此类模拟系统的设计选择。我们的分析揭示了关于语言模型是否以及如何用于模拟人类的问题，并表明大语言模型（Large Language Models, LLMs）在描述观点分布方面比模拟这些分布更为准确。

[NLP-29] owards Low-Resource Harmful Meme Detection with LMM Agents EMNLP2024

【速读】： 该论文试图解决在社交媒体时代，由于模因（memes）的动态特性，现有数据驱动模型在低资源场景下（即仅有少量标注样本）难以有效识别有害模因的问题。解决方案的关键在于提出了一种机构驱动的框架，通过少量样本标注进行内外部分析。具体来说，该框架利用大型多模态模型（Large Multimodal Models, LMMs）的能力，首先检索并利用带有标注的相关模因作为辅助信号，然后激发LMMs内部的认知修正行为，以获得对模因有害性的广义洞察。通过结合这些策略，该方法能够对复杂和隐含的有害模式进行辩证推理，从而在低资源有害模因检测任务中显著优于现有最先进的方法。

Abstract:The proliferation of Internet memes in the age of social media necessitates effective identification of harmful ones. Due to the dynamic nature of memes, existing data-driven models may struggle in low-resource scenarios where only a few labeled examples are available. In this paper, we propose an agency-driven framework for low-resource harmful meme detection, employing both outward and inward analysis with few-shot annotated samples. Inspired by the powerful capacity of Large Multimodal Models (LMMs) on multimodal reasoning, we first retrieve relative memes with annotations to leverage label information as auxiliary signals for the LMM agent. Then, we elicit knowledge-revising behavior within the LMM agent to derive well-generalized insights into meme harmfulness. By combining these strategies, our approach enables dialectical reasoning over intricate and implicit harm-indicative patterns. Extensive experiments conducted on three meme datasets demonstrate that our proposed approach achieves superior performance than state-of-the-art methods on the low-resource harmful meme detection task.

[NLP-30] Word reuse and combination support efficient communication of emerging concepts

【速读】： 该论文试图解决词汇表达新概念（lexicalization）过程中两种主要策略——词汇重用（word reuse）和词汇组合（word combination）之间的权衡问题。解决方案的关键在于提出了一个基于信息论的统一框架，该框架揭示了这两种策略如何在保持词汇形式长度（word length）和提高信息精确度（precision）之间进行权衡。具体来说，词汇重用倾向于保持词汇的平均长度，但牺牲了一定的精确度；而词汇组合则倾向于生成更具信息量的词汇，但代价是词汇长度增加。通过对比英语、法语和芬兰语在过去一个世纪中的实际词汇重用和组合数据，研究发现这些历史上的词汇策略在沟通效率上优于假设的词汇构建方式，并且字面意义的词汇重用和组合通常比非字面意义的更高效。这一结果支持了词汇重用和组合策略在基于有效沟通理论的词汇化过程中的一致性。

链接: https://arxiv.org/abs/2411.05379
作者: Aotao Xu,Charles Kemp,Lea Frermann,Yang Xu
关键词-EN: key function, express novel concepts, emerge over time, word, common lexicalization strategies
类目: Computation and Language (cs.CL)
备注: Published in Proceedings of the National Academy of Sciences

点击查看摘要

Abstract:A key function of the lexicon is to express novel concepts as they emerge over time through a process known as lexicalization. The most common lexicalization strategies are the reuse and combination of existing words, but they have typically been studied separately in the areas of word meaning extension and word formation. Here we offer an information-theoretic account of how both strategies are constrained by a fundamental tradeoff between competing communicative pressures: word reuse tends to preserve the average length of word forms at the cost of less precision, while word combination tends to produce more informative words at the expense of greater word length. We test our proposal against a large dataset of reuse items and compounds that appeared in English, French and Finnish over the past century. We find that these historically emerging items achieve higher levels of communicative efficiency than hypothetical ways of constructing the lexicon, and both literal reuse items and compounds tend to be more efficient than their non-literal counterparts. These results suggest that reuse and combination are both consistent with a unified account of lexicalization grounded in the theory of efficient communication.
摘要：词汇的一个关键功能是通过一个称为词汇化的过程来表达随着时间出现的新的概念。最常见的词汇化策略是重复使用和组合现有的词语，但它们通常在词义扩展和词形成领域分别进行研究。在这里，我们提供了一个基于信息理论的解释，说明这两种策略如何受到基本权衡的制约：词语重复使用倾向于保持词语形式的平均长度，但代价是精确度较低；而词语组合则倾向于产生更具信息量的词语，但代价是词语长度增加。我们针对过去一个世纪在英语、法语和芬兰语中出现的大量重复使用和复合词数据集测试了我们的提议。我们发现，这些历史上出现的词汇化项目在交流效率上高于假设的词汇构建方式，并且重复使用的词汇和复合词往往比非重复使用的词汇更有效。这些结果表明，重复使用和组合都与基于高效交流理论的词汇化统一解释相一致。

[NLP-31] Ev2R: Evaluating Evidence Retrieval in Automated Fact-Checking

【速读】： 该论文试图解决自动化事实核查 (Automated Fact-Checking, AFC) 中证据评估方法的局限性问题，这些方法通常依赖于预定义的封闭知识源（如Wikipedia）或通过预测裁决隐式评估证据。论文提出的解决方案是引入Ev2R框架，该框架包含三种证据评估方法：基于参考的评估、代理参考评估和无参考评估。关键在于利用自然语言生成 (Natural Language Generation, NLG) 评估的最新进展，特别是通过提示 (prompt) 驱动的评分器，尤其是那些利用大型语言模型 (Large Language Models, LLMs) 和参考证据的评分器，以提高评估效果。实验结果表明，这些方法在人类评级和对抗测试中的表现优于传统评估方法。

链接: https://arxiv.org/abs/2411.05375
作者: Mubashara Akhtar,Michael Schlichtkrull,Andreas Vlachos
关键词-EN: Current automated fact-checking, Current automated, closed knowledge source, predefined closed knowledge, comparing retrieved evidence
类目: Computation and Language (cs.CL); Artificial Intelligence (cs.AI); Information Retrieval (cs.IR); Machine Learning (cs.LG)
备注: 10 pages

点击查看摘要

Abstract:Current automated fact-checking (AFC) approaches commonly evaluate evidence either implicitly via the predicted verdicts or by comparing retrieved evidence with a predefined closed knowledge source, such as Wikipedia. However, these methods suffer from limitations, resulting from their reliance on evaluation metrics developed for different purposes and constraints imposed by closed knowledge sources. Recent advances in natural language generation (NLG) evaluation offer new possibilities for evidence assessment. In this work, we introduce Ev2R, an evaluation framework for AFC that comprises three types of approaches for evidence evaluation: reference-based, proxy-reference, and reference-less. We evaluate their effectiveness through agreement with human ratings and adversarial tests, and demonstrate that prompt-based scorers, particularly those leveraging LLMs and reference evidence, outperform traditional evaluation approaches.
摘要：当前的自动化事实核查 (Automated Fact-Checking, AFC) 方法通常通过预测的判决结果或通过将检索到的证据与预定义的封闭知识源（如 Wikipedia）进行比较来隐式评估证据。然而，这些方法存在局限性，主要源于它们依赖于为不同目的开发的评估指标以及封闭知识源的限制。自然语言生成 (Natural Language Generation, NLG) 评估领域的最新进展为证据评估提供了新的可能性。在本研究中，我们提出了 Ev2R，这是一个用于 AFC 的评估框架，包含三种类型的证据评估方法：基于参考的、代理参考的和无参考的。我们通过与人类评分的共识和对抗性测试来评估它们的效果，并证明基于提示的评分器，特别是那些利用大语言模型 (Large Language Model, LLM) 和参考证据的评分器，优于传统的评估方法。

[NLP-32] Dynamic-SUPERB Phase-2: A Collaboratively Expanding Benchmark for Measuring the Capabilities of Spoken Language Models with 180 Tasks

Abstract:Multimodal foundation models, such as Gemini and ChatGPT, have revolutionized human-machine interactions by seamlessly integrating various forms of data. Developing a universal spoken language model that comprehends a wide range of natural language instructions is critical for bridging communication gaps and facilitating more intuitive interactions. However, the absence of a comprehensive evaluation benchmark poses a significant challenge. We present Dynamic-SUPERB Phase-2, an open and evolving benchmark for the comprehensive evaluation of instruction-based universal speech models. Building upon the first generation, this second version incorporates 125 new tasks contributed collaboratively by the global research community, expanding the benchmark to a total of 180 tasks, making it the largest benchmark for speech and audio evaluation. While the first generation of Dynamic-SUPERB was limited to classification tasks, Dynamic-SUPERB Phase-2 broadens its evaluation capabilities by introducing a wide array of novel and diverse tasks, including regression and sequence generation, across speech, music, and environmental audio. Evaluation results indicate that none of the models performed well universally. SALMONN-13B excelled in English ASR, while WavLLM demonstrated high accuracy in emotion recognition, but current models still require further innovations to handle a broader range of tasks. We will soon open-source all task data and the evaluation pipeline.
摘要：多模态基础模型，如 Gemini 和 ChatGPT，通过无缝整合多种数据形式，彻底改变了人机交互方式。开发一个能够理解广泛自然语言指令的通用口语语言模型，对于弥合沟通鸿沟和促进更直观的交互至关重要。然而，缺乏一个全面的评估基准构成了重大挑战。我们提出了 Dynamic-SUPERB 第二阶段，这是一个开放且不断发展的基准，用于全面评估基于指令的通用语音模型。基于第一代，第二版本纳入了全球研究社区共同贡献的 125 项新任务，使基准任务总数扩展至 180 项，成为语音和音频评估领域最大的基准。虽然第一代 Dynamic-SUPERB 仅限于分类任务，但 Dynamic-SUPERB 第二阶段通过引入大量新颖且多样化的任务，扩展了其评估能力，包括回归和序列生成任务，涵盖语音、音乐和环境音频。评估结果显示，没有任何模型在所有任务中表现出色。SALMONN-13B 在英语自动语音识别（ASR）中表现优异，而 WavLLM 在情感识别中展示了高准确率，但当前模型仍需进一步创新以应对更广泛的任务范围。我们即将开源所有任务数据和评估流程。

[NLP-33] Reasoning Robustness of LLM s to Adversarial Typographical Errors

【速读】： 该论文试图解决大型语言模型（LLMs）在面对用户查询中的拼写错误时推理鲁棒性的问题。解决方案的关键在于设计了一种对抗性拼写错误攻击算法（Adversarial Typo Attack, ATA），该算法通过迭代地对查询中关键单词进行拼写错误采样，并选择最有可能成功攻击的编辑方式，从而评估LLMs对拼写错误的敏感性。实验结果表明，即使是最小的拼写错误（1个字符编辑）也能显著降低Mistral-7B-Instruct在GSM8K数据集上的准确率，从43.7%降至38.6%，而8个字符编辑则进一步降至19.2%。此外，论文还开发了R²ATA基准，用于评估更大规模和闭源LLMs的推理鲁棒性，展示了该方法在不同LLMs之间的显著转移性和性能下降。

链接: https://arxiv.org/abs/2411.05345
作者: Esther Gan,Yiran Zhao,Liying Cheng,Yancan Mao,Anirudh Goyal,Kenji Kawaguchi,Min-Yen Kan,Michael Shieh
关键词-EN: Large Language Models, Language Models, demonstrated impressive capabilities, Large Language, ATA
类目: Computation and Language (cs.CL); Artificial Intelligence (cs.AI)
备注:

点击查看摘要

Abstract:Large Language Models (LLMs) have demonstrated impressive capabilities in reasoning using Chain-of-Thought (CoT) prompting. However, CoT can be biased by users’ instruction. In this work, we study the reasoning robustness of LLMs to typographical errors, which can naturally occur in users’ queries. We design an Adversarial Typo Attack ( \textttATA ) algorithm that iteratively samples typos for words that are important to the query and selects the edit that is most likely to succeed in attacking. It shows that LLMs are sensitive to minimal adversarial typographical changes. Notably, with 1 character edit, Mistral-7B-Instruct’s accuracy drops from 43.7% to 38.6% on GSM8K, while with 8 character edits the performance further drops to 19.2%. To extend our evaluation to larger and closed-source LLMs, we develop the \textttR ^2 ATA benchmark, which assesses models’ \underlineR easoning \underlineR obustness to \underline\textttATA . It includes adversarial typographical questions derived from three widely used reasoning datasets-GSM8K, BBH, and MMLU-by applying \textttATA to open-source LLMs. \textttR ^2 ATA demonstrates remarkable transferability and causes notable performance drops across multiple super large and closed-source LLMs.
摘要：大语言模型 (LLMs) 在利用思维链 (Chain-of-Thought, CoT) 提示进行推理方面展示了令人印象深刻的能力。然而，CoT 可能会受到用户指令的偏见影响。在本研究中，我们探讨了 LLMs 对用户查询中自然出现的拼写错误的推理鲁棒性。我们设计了一种对抗性拼写错误攻击算法 (Adversarial Typo Attack, ATA)，该算法迭代地对查询中重要的词汇进行拼写错误采样，并选择最有可能成功攻击的编辑。结果显示，LLMs 对微小的对抗性拼写变化非常敏感。值得注意的是，仅通过一个字符的编辑，Mistral-7B-Instruct 在 GSM8K 上的准确率从 43.7% 下降到 38.6%，而通过 8 个字符的编辑，性能进一步下降到 19.2%。为了将我们的评估扩展到更大且闭源的 LLMs，我们开发了 R²ATA 基准测试，该基准测试评估模型对 ATA 的推理鲁棒性。它包括通过将 ATA 应用于开源 LLMs 而得出的来自三个广泛使用的推理数据集（GSM8K、BBH 和 MMLU）的对抗性拼写错误问题。R²ATA 展示了显著的可迁移性，并导致多个超大型和闭源 LLMs 的性能显著下降。

[NLP-34] Improving Multi-Domain Task-Oriented Dialogue System with Offline Reinforcement Learning

【速读】： 该论文试图解决面向任务的对话系统 (Task-oriented Dialogue, TOD) 中存在的暴露偏差 (exposure bias) 和令牌损失 (token loss) 问题，这些问题导致模型偏离用户任务的完成。解决方案的关键在于利用统一的预训练语言模型 GPT2，并通过监督学习 (supervised learning) 和强化学习 (reinforcement learning, RL) 进行优化。具体来说，通过引入不可微分的奖励函数，结合成功率和 BLEU 评估指标的加权和来计算奖励，从而指导语言模型生成既符合任务要求又连贯流畅的响应。实验结果表明，该方法在 MultiWOZ2.1 数据集上显著提升了信息传递率和成功率。

链接: https://arxiv.org/abs/2411.05340
作者: Dharmendra Prajapat,Durga Toshniwal
关键词-EN: Task-oriented dialogue, accomplish user-defined tasks, TOD system, TOD, designed to accomplish
类目: Computation and Language (cs.CL); Artificial Intelligence (cs.AI); Human-Computer Interaction (cs.HC); Information Retrieval (cs.IR)
备注:

点击查看摘要

Abstract:Task-oriented dialogue (TOD) system is designed to accomplish user-defined tasks through dialogues. The TOD system has progressed towards end-to-end modeling by leveraging pre-trained large language models. Fine-tuning the pre-trained language models using only supervised learning leads to the exposure bias and token loss problem and it deviates the models from completing the user’s task. To address these issues, we propose a TOD system that leverages a unified pre-trained language model, GPT2, as a base model. It is optimized using supervised learning and reinforcement learning (RL). The issues in the TOD system are mitigated using a non-differentiable reward function. The reward is calculated using the weighted sum of the success rate and BLEU evaluation metrics. The success rate and BLEU metrics in reward calculation guide the language model for user task completion while ensuring a coherent and fluent response. Our model is acquired by fine-tuning a pre-trained model on the dialogue-session level which comprises user utterance, belief state, system act, and system response. Experimental results on MultiWOZ2.1 demonstrate that our model increases the inform rate by 1.60% and the success rate by 3.17% compared to the baseline.
摘要：面向任务的对话 (Task-oriented Dialogue, TOD) 系统旨在通过对话完成用户定义的任务。TOD 系统通过利用预训练的大语言模型，已经向端到端建模方向发展。仅使用监督学习对预训练语言模型进行微调会导致暴露偏差和 Token 损失问题，并使模型偏离完成用户任务的目标。为了解决这些问题，我们提出了一种利用统一预训练语言模型 GPT2 作为基础模型的 TOD 系统。该系统通过监督学习和强化学习 (Reinforcement Learning, RL) 进行优化。通过使用不可微分的奖励函数来缓解 TOD 系统中的问题。奖励计算采用成功率和 BLEU 评估指标的加权和。成功率和 BLEU 指标在奖励计算中指导语言模型完成用户任务，同时确保响应的连贯性和流畅性。我们的模型通过对包含用户话语、信念状态、系统行为和系统响应的对话会话级别的预训练模型进行微调获得。在 MultiWOZ2.1 数据集上的实验结果表明，与基线模型相比，我们的模型将信息率提高了 1.60%，成功率提高了 3.17%。

Abstract:Scientific literature is typically dense, requiring significant background knowledge and deep comprehension for effective engagement. We introduce SciDQA, a new dataset for reading comprehension that challenges LLMs for a deep understanding of scientific articles, consisting of 2,937 QA pairs. Unlike other scientific QA datasets, SciDQA sources questions from peer reviews by domain experts and answers by paper authors, ensuring a thorough examination of the literature. We enhance the dataset’s quality through a process that carefully filters out lower quality questions, decontextualizes the content, tracks the source document across different versions, and incorporates a bibliography for multi-document question-answering. Questions in SciDQA necessitate reasoning across figures, tables, equations, appendices, and supplementary materials, and require multi-document reasoning. We evaluate several open-source and proprietary LLMs across various configurations to explore their capabilities in generating relevant and factual responses. Our comprehensive evaluation, based on metrics for surface-level similarity and LLM judgements, highlights notable performance discrepancies. SciDQA represents a rigorously curated, naturally derived scientific QA dataset, designed to facilitate research on complex scientific text understanding.
摘要：科学文献通常内容密集，需要丰富的背景知识和深入的理解才能有效参与。我们引入了 SciDQA，这是一个用于阅读理解的新数据集，旨在挑战大语言模型对科学文章的深入理解，该数据集包含 2,937 个问答对。与其它科学问答数据集不同，SciDQA 的问题来源于领域专家的同行评审，答案则由论文作者提供，确保了对文献的全面考察。我们通过一个精心设计的流程来提升数据集的质量，该流程包括筛选低质量问题、去上下文化内容、跟踪不同版本中的源文档，并引入参考文献以支持多文档问答。SciDQA 中的问题需要跨图表、表格、方程式、附录和补充材料进行推理，并要求多文档推理。我们评估了多种开源和专有大语言模型在不同配置下的表现，以探索它们生成相关且事实性响应的能力。基于表面相似度和大语言模型判断的综合评估，揭示了显著的性能差异。SciDQA 是一个经过严格筛选、自然生成的科学问答数据集，旨在促进复杂科学文本理解的研究。

[NLP-36] SpecHub: Provable Acceleration to Multi-Draft Speculative Decoding EMNLP2024

【速读】： 该论文试图解决大语言模型 (Large Language Models, LLMs) 在自然语言处理 (Natural Language Processing, NLP) 任务中因顺序生成令牌 (token) 而导致的推理速度受限问题。解决方案的关键在于提出了一种名为 SpecHub 的新型高效采样-验证方法，用于多草稿推测解码 (Multi-Draft Speculative Decoding, MDSD)。SpecHub 通过将最优传输问题 (Optimal Transport with Membership Cost, OTM) 简化为紧凑的线性规划模型 (Linear Programming model)，显著降低了计算复杂度，并利用稀疏联合分布 (sparse joint distribution) 加速采样过程，从而在保持线性计算开销的同时提高了接受率 (acceptance rates)。实验结果表明，SpecHub 在每一步生成中比现有的递归拒绝采样 (Recursive Rejection Sampling, RRS) 方法多生成 0.05-0.27 和 0.02-0.16 个令牌。

链接: https://arxiv.org/abs/2411.05289
作者: Ryan Sun,Tianyi Zhou,Xun Chen,Lichao Sun
关键词-EN: Large Language Models, natural language processing, advancing natural language, Large Language, limits inference speed
类目: Computation and Language (cs.CL); Artificial Intelligence (cs.AI)
备注: EMNLP 2024 (Main)

点击查看摘要

Abstract:Large Language Models (LLMs) have become essential in advancing natural language processing (NLP) tasks, but their sequential token generation limits inference speed. Multi-Draft Speculative Decoding (MDSD) offers a promising solution by using a smaller draft model to generate multiple token sequences, which the target LLM verifies in parallel. However, current heuristic approaches, such as Recursive Rejection Sampling (RRS), suffer from low acceptance rates in subsequent drafts, limiting the advantages of using multiple drafts. Meanwhile, Optimal Transport with Membership Cost (OTM) can theoretically improve acceptance rates, but its computational cost is too high for real-time use. We present SpecHub, a novel, efficient sampling-verification method for MDSD that improves acceptance rates with only linear computational overhead. By simplifying the OTM problem into a compact Linear Programming model, SpecHub significantly reduces computational complexity. It further accelerates sampling by leveraging a sparse joint distribution, focusing computation on high-probability token sequences. In extensive experiments, Spechub consistently generates 0.05-0.27 and 0.02-0.16 more tokens per step than RRS and RRS without replacement. We attach our code at \urlthis https URL.
摘要：大语言模型（LLMs）在推动自然语言处理（NLP）任务方面已成为不可或缺的工具，但其逐个生成 Token 的方式限制了推理速度。多草稿推测解码（Multi-Draft Speculative Decoding, MDSD）通过使用较小的草稿模型生成多个 Token 序列，并由目标 LLM 并行验证，提供了一个有前景的解决方案。然而，当前的启发式方法，如递归拒绝采样（Recursive Rejection Sampling, RRS），在后续草稿中的接受率较低，限制了使用多草稿的优势。同时，基于成员成本的最优传输（Optimal Transport with Membership Cost, OTM）理论上可以提高接受率，但其计算成本过高，无法实时应用。我们提出了 SpecHub，一种新颖且高效的采样-验证方法，用于 MDSD，能够在仅增加线性计算开销的情况下提高接受率。通过将 OTM 问题简化为紧凑的线性规划模型，SpecHub 显著降低了计算复杂度。此外，它通过利用稀疏联合分布，将计算集中在高概率 Token 序列上，进一步加速了采样过程。在广泛的实验中，SpecHub 在每一步生成的 Token 数量上，分别比 RRS 和无替换的 RRS 多出 0.05-0.27 和 0.02-0.16。我们附上了代码链接 \urlthis https URL。

[NLP-37] Fox-1 Technical Report

【速读】： 该论文试图解决小语言模型（SLMs）在预训练效率和性能上的问题。解决方案的关键在于引入了一种新颖的三阶段数据课程（3-stage data curriculum），通过在2K-8K序列长度上进行训练，提高了预训练效率。此外，Fox-1模型在架构设计上采用了更深的层结构、扩展的词汇表以及Grouped Query Attention (GQA)，从而在性能和效率上优于其他SLMs。通过这些创新，Fox-1在多个基准测试中表现优于或与StableLM-2-1.6B、Gemma-2B、Qwen1.5-1.8B和OpenELM1.1B相当，同时保持了竞争性的推理速度和吞吐量。

链接: https://arxiv.org/abs/2411.05281
作者: Zijian Hu,Jipeng Zhang,Rui Pan,Zhaozhuo Xu,Salman Avestimehr,Chaoyang He,Tong Zhang
关键词-EN: small language models, series of small, small language, Grouped Query Attention, language models
类目: Computation and Language (cs.CL); Artificial Intelligence (cs.AI); Machine Learning (cs.LG)
备注: Base model is available at this https URL and the instruction-tuned version is available at this https URL

Abstract:We present Fox-1, a series of small language models (SLMs) consisting of Fox-1-1.6B and Fox-1-1.6B-Instruct-v0.1. These models are pre-trained on 3 trillion tokens of web-scraped document data and fine-tuned with 5 billion tokens of instruction-following and multi-turn conversation data. Aiming to improve the pre-training efficiency, Fox-1-1.6B model introduces a novel 3-stage data curriculum across all the training data with 2K-8K sequence length. In architecture design, Fox-1 features a deeper layer structure, an expanded vocabulary, and utilizes Grouped Query Attention (GQA), offering a performant and efficient architecture compared to other SLMs. Fox-1 achieves better or on-par performance in various benchmarks compared to StableLM-2-1.6B, Gemma-2B, Qwen1.5-1.8B, and OpenELM1.1B, with competitive inference speed and throughput. The model weights have been released under the Apache 2.0 license, where we aim to promote the democratization of LLMs and make them fully accessible to the whole open-source community.
摘要：我们介绍了 Fox-1，这是一系列小型语言模型 (SLM)，包括 Fox-1-1.6B 和 Fox-1-1.6B-Instruct-v0.1。这些模型在 3 万亿个 Token 的网络抓取文档数据上进行了预训练，并使用 50 亿个 Token 的指令跟随和多轮对话数据进行了微调。为了提高预训练效率，Fox-1-1.6B 模型引入了一种新颖的 3 阶段数据课程，涵盖了所有训练数据，序列长度为 2K-8K。在架构设计方面，Fox-1 采用了更深的层结构、扩展的词汇表，并利用了分组查询注意力 (Grouped Query Attention, GQA)，与其他 SLM 相比，提供了性能更高且更高效的架构。在各种基准测试中，Fox-1 的表现优于或与 StableLM-2-1.6B、Gemma-2B、Qwen1.5-1.8B 和 OpenELM1.1B 相当，同时具有竞争力的推理速度和吞吐量。模型权重已在 Apache 2.0 许可证下发布，我们的目标是促进大语言模型 (LLM) 的民主化，使其完全可被整个开源社区访问。

[NLP-38] Revisiting the Robustness of Watermarking to Paraphrasing Attacks EMNLP2024

【速读】： 该论文试图解决的问题是现有文本水印技术在面对改写（paraphrasing）攻击时的脆弱性。尽管一些水印技术声称对改写具有鲁棒性，但论文指出这些技术并未充分考虑到其容易被逆向工程破解的弱点。解决方案的关键在于揭示了仅通过有限数量的生成文本，攻击者就能显著提高改写攻击的有效性，从而绕过水印检测，使水印失效。

链接: https://arxiv.org/abs/2411.05277
作者: Saksham Rastogi,Danish Pruthi
关键词-EN: Amidst rising concerns, Amidst rising, rising concerns, internet being proliferated, proliferated with content
类目: Cryptography and Security (cs.CR); Computation and Language (cs.CL); Machine Learning (cs.LG)
备注: EMNLP 2024

点击查看摘要

Abstract:Amidst rising concerns about the internet being proliferated with content generated from language models (LMs), watermarking is seen as a principled way to certify whether text was generated from a model. Many recent watermarking techniques slightly modify the output probabilities of LMs to embed a signal in the generated output that can later be detected. Since early proposals for text watermarking, questions about their robustness to paraphrasing have been prominently discussed. Lately, some techniques are deliberately designed and claimed to be robust to paraphrasing. However, such watermarking schemes do not adequately account for the ease with which they can be reverse-engineered. We show that with access to only a limited number of generations from a black-box watermarked model, we can drastically increase the effectiveness of paraphrasing attacks to evade watermark detection, thereby rendering the watermark ineffective.
摘要：随着人们对互联网上充斥着由语言模型 (LMs) 生成的内容的担忧日益增加，水印技术被视为一种原则性的方法，用于认证文本是否由模型生成。许多最近的水印技术通过略微修改 LMs 的输出概率，在生成的输出中嵌入一个信号，该信号可以在之后被检测到。自早期提出文本水印技术以来，关于其对改写 (paraphrasing) 的鲁棒性的问题一直备受关注。最近，一些技术被特意设计和声称对改写具有鲁棒性。然而，这些水印方案并未充分考虑到它们容易被逆向工程的便利性。我们表明，仅通过访问少量来自黑箱水印模型的生成内容，我们就能显著提高改写攻击的有效性，从而逃避水印检测，使得水印失效。

[NLP-39] Seeing Through the Fog: A Cost-Effectiveness Analysis of Hallucination Detection Systems

Abstract:This paper presents a comparative analysis of hallucination detection systems for AI, focusing on automatic summarization and question answering tasks for Large Language Models (LLMs). We evaluate different hallucination detection systems using the diagnostic odds ratio (DOR) and cost-effectiveness metrics. Our results indicate that although advanced models can perform better they come at a much higher cost. We also demonstrate how an ideal hallucination detection system needs to maintain performance across different model sizes. Our findings highlight the importance of choosing a detection system aligned with specific application needs and resource constraints. Future research will explore hybrid systems and automated identification of underperforming components to enhance AI reliability and efficiency in detecting and mitigating hallucinations.
摘要：本文对用于人工智能的幻觉检测系统进行了比较分析，重点研究了大语言模型 (LLM) 在自动摘要和问答任务中的应用。我们使用诊断优势比 (DOR) 和成本效益指标评估了不同的幻觉检测系统。结果表明，尽管高级模型可以表现更好，但其成本显著增加。我们还展示了理想的幻觉检测系统如何在不同模型规模下保持性能。研究结果强调了选择与特定应用需求和资源限制相匹配的检测系统的重要性。未来的研究将探索混合系统以及自动化识别表现不佳的组件，以提高人工智能在检测和缓解幻觉方面的可靠性和效率。

Abstract:Large language models (LLMs) have shown remarkable performance across various tasks, yet their ability to handle long-context reading remains challenging. This study explores the effectiveness of leveraging high-quality academic peer review data for fine-tuning LLMs to enhance their long-context capabilities. We compare the Direct Preference Optimization (DPO) method with the Supervised Fine-Tuning (SFT) method, demonstrating DPO’s superiority and data efficiency. Additionally, the zero-shot benchmark results indicate that aggregated high-quality human reviews are overwhelmingly preferred over LLM-generated responses, even for the most capable models like GPT-4o. This suggests that high-quality human reviews are extremely rich in information, reasoning, and long-context retrieval, capabilities that even the most advanced models have not fully captured. These findings highlight the high utility of leveraging human reviews to further advance the field. Abstract:Computational narrative understanding studies the identification, description, and interaction of the elements of a narrative: characters, attributes, events, and relations. Narrative research has given considerable attention to defining and classifying character types. Our work addresses this by curating the Chatter dataset that labels whether a character portrays some attribute for 88148 character-attribute pairs, encompassing 2998 characters, 13324 attributes and 660 movies. [NLP-45] Beyond the Numbers: Transparency in Relation Extraction Benchmark Creation and Leaderboards EMNLP2024

【速读】： 该论文试图解决自然语言处理 (NLP) 领域中关系抽取 (Relation Extraction, RE) 任务的基准测试和排行榜透明度不足的问题。论文指出，现有的 RE 基准测试在数据来源、标注一致性、数据选择算法和潜在偏差（如数据不平衡）等方面缺乏详细的文档记录，导致对模型真实泛化能力的评估不准确。解决方案的关键在于提高基准测试的文档透明度，包括详细记录数据来源和处理过程，以及采用更严格的评估方法，如引入基于类别的性能指标，以更准确地反映模型在多关系类型数据集上的表现。此外，论文建议在报告 RE 任务进展时，应更加关注这些透明度和评估方法的改进，以推动该领域的发展。

链接: https://arxiv.org/abs/2411.05224
作者: Varvara Arzt,Allan Hanbury
关键词-EN: measuring progress, benchmarks, relation extraction, investigates the transparency, paper investigates
类目: Computation and Language (cs.CL)
备注: This paper was accepted at the GenBench workshop at EMNLP2024

点击查看摘要

Abstract:This paper investigates the transparency in the creation of benchmarks and the use of leaderboards for measuring progress in NLP, with a focus on the relation extraction (RE) task. Existing RE benchmarks often suffer from insufficient documentation, lacking crucial details such as data sources, inter-annotator agreement, the algorithms used for the selection of instances for datasets, and information on potential biases like dataset imbalance. Progress in RE is frequently measured by leaderboards that rank systems based on evaluation methods, typically limited to aggregate metrics like F1-score. However, the absence of detailed performance analysis beyond these metrics can obscure the true generalisation capabilities of models. Our analysis reveals that widely used RE benchmarks, such as TACRED and NYT, tend to be highly imbalanced and contain noisy labels. Moreover, the lack of class-based performance metrics fails to accurately reflect model performance across datasets with a large number of relation types. These limitations should be carefully considered when reporting progress in RE. While our discussion centers on the transparency of RE benchmarks and leaderboards, the observations we discuss are broadly applicable to other NLP tasks as well. Rather than undermining the significance and value of existing RE benchmarks and the development of new models, this paper advocates for improved documentation and more rigorous evaluation to advance the field.
摘要：本文探讨了在自然语言处理（NLP）领域中，用于衡量关系抽取（Relation Extraction, RE）任务进展的基准创建透明度及排行榜使用情况。现有的 RE 基准往往存在文档不足的问题，缺乏关键细节，如数据来源、标注者间的一致性、用于数据集实例选择的算法，以及潜在偏差信息（如数据集不平衡）。RE 领域的进展通常通过排行榜来衡量，这些排行榜根据评估方法对系统进行排名，通常仅限于 F1-score 等综合指标。然而，这些指标之外的详细性能分析缺失，可能会掩盖模型的真实泛化能力。我们的分析显示，广泛使用的 RE 基准（如 TACRED 和 NYT）往往高度不平衡且包含噪声标签。此外，缺乏基于类别的性能指标无法准确反映模型在包含大量关系类型的数据集上的表现。在报告 RE 进展时，应仔细考虑这些局限性。尽管我们的讨论集中于 RE 基准和排行榜的透明度，但我们所讨论的观察结果同样适用于其他 NLP 任务。本文并非削弱现有 RE 基准和新模型开发的重要性与价值，而是主张通过改进文档和更严格的评估来推动该领域的发展。

[NLP-46] STAND-Guard: A Small Task-Adaptive Content Moderation Model

【速读】： 该论文试图解决内容审核任务的适应性问题，即如何在不进行大量模型调整的情况下，使模型能够准确适应新的或定制化的内容审核任务。解决方案的关键在于提出了STAND-GUARD模型，这是一个小型任务自适应内容审核模型。通过在多种内容审核任务上进行指令微调（instruct tuning），STAND-GUARD能够释放小型语言模型（SLMs）在未见（out-of-distribution）内容审核任务上的潜力。论文还研究了训练任务和模型大小对跨任务微调机制效果的影响，实验结果表明STAND-GUARD在超过40个公共数据集和来自真实商业场景的专有数据集上与GPT-3.5-Turbo表现相当，甚至在未见英语二分类任务上接近GPT-4-Turbo的效果。

Abstract:Content moderation, the process of reviewing and monitoring the safety of generated content, is important for development of welcoming online platforms and responsible large language models. Content moderation contains various tasks, each with its unique requirements tailored to specific scenarios. Therefore, it is crucial to develop a model that can be easily adapted to novel or customized content moderation tasks accurately without extensive model tuning. This paper presents STAND-GUARD, a Small Task-Adaptive coNtent moDeration model. The basic motivation is: by performing instruct tuning on various content moderation tasks, we can unleash the power of small language models (SLMs) on unseen (out-of-distribution) content moderation tasks. We also carefully study the effects of training tasks and model size on the efficacy of cross-task fine-tuning mechanism. Experiments demonstrate STAND-Guard is comparable to GPT-3.5-Turbo across over 40 public datasets, as well as proprietary datasets derived from real-world business scenarios. [NLP-47] Alopex: A Computational Framework for Enabling On-Device Function Calls with LLM s

【速读】： 该论文试图解决在移动设备上集成大型语言模型（Large Language Models, LLMs）时面临的挑战，包括数据稀缺、问题格式不当以及灾难性遗忘（catastrophic forgetting）等问题。解决方案的关键在于提出了Alopex框架，该框架通过以下几个关键技术来解决这些问题：1) 引入基于逻辑的方法生成高质量的训练数据；2) 采用新颖的“描述-问题-输出”格式进行微调，以减少函数信息泄露的风险；3) 使用数据混合策略，将函数调用数据与教科书数据集结合，以缓解灾难性遗忘问题，从而提升模型在多种任务中的表现。实验结果表明，Alopex显著提高了函数调用的准确性，并有效减少了灾难性遗忘，为在LLMs中集成函数调用能力提供了一个无需人工干预的稳健解决方案。
